The Life of Littletato



Synopsis: This story talks about The Life of Littletato, a potato that always loved traveling, she got that from her father.
She lived traveling between cities after she reached nineteen.
And stopped on a city to look, it was San Francisco, she met another potato there.
They started to talk, know each other a little more, and the life of Littletato started to change.

You are reading: The Life of Littletato
Chapter: 1 - The Beginning, Part One






Hello, I am Izaque Sanvezzo, Stake2, and Funkysnipa Cat.

This is "The Life of Littletato", a story of mine, I created on August 5, 2017 (05/08/2017).
I created it on the "Wattpad" story website, it was one of my first stories.
It came after my first story, "Desert Island", created on October 23, 2016 (23/10/2016).
I created an account on Wattpad and wanted to test the website, and how it would be to write on it, creating a story called "Littletato".
Which was a mix of "Little" and "Potato", then, I began to write it.
I wrote an entire chapter in one line, with grammatical and typographical errors, with few interesting things.
I still have files of the old chapters to read and see how my writing and storytelling skills have improved.
So, in 2021, I started to revise all of the chapters, to make them better.
And write them in the style of my story "SpaceLiving", with topics and transitions separated by paragraphs.
My story "SpaceLiving" was created on January 19, 2019 (19/01/2019).
I got inspired to start writing stories because of a Brazilian story in the green text format, a writing style that originated on the website 4chan.
The story is called "Year 2035", a name given by me, as it is the first sentence of the story.
Created by "Magno A Lima", around 2017, it is a story of science fiction, survival, fighting, zombies, and superpowers.
It tells the story of "Andros", a man who participates in resistance, fighting against a controlling government.
Against zombies, controlling corporations, criminals, and scientific experiments on humans.
The story was so good and interesting, I could feel what the characters were feeling, and imagine the scenes and scenarios.
And I wanted to make people feel and imagine that too, that is why I started writing Littletato.
It has been six years already, six years of writing Littletato, this wonderful story, I am writing from 2023.
It is incredible to see how Littletato has evolved a lot over these six years.
She started as a potato, and a story of a potato in a world of vegetables, like a fable, and a test story.
And she evolved into a girl, a responsible and mature woman, who has her house, work, and a spouse.
She has fun, listens to music, watches things, rides a car, visits places, and goes out with her friends.
I am so happy to know that I already created thirty-three chapters of this story, that makes me so happy :3.
I love this story so much, it helped me create this love and passion for writing and helped me start writing other stories of mine too, like SpaceLiving.
So, thanks for giving my story a try, and I hope you enjoy reading it as much as I enjoyed writing it.

This story is inspired by:
Slice of life anime, that shows the everyday life of a person.
The anime "Yuru Camp", shows the lives of girls who like to camp as a pastime and their daily lives.
It is a very relaxing anime about camping, and it has a very relaxing soundtrack too, which I always listen to while writing Littletato.
I would say that the soundtrack of Littletato is the soundtrack of Yuru Camp, and also songs from the folk genre.
Littletato would also like to go camping just like the girls of the anime.
She likes to have relaxing moments like this, on a Saturday morning, after having lunch, spending time with her family or friends, sitting on the sofa.
Watching TV, sitting on area chairs, relaxing, in a park having a picnic, or going on a trip.
This story is also inspired by normal daily life, that I have, and that I see in other places.
For example, in various media, anime, cartoons, series, movies, and videos that show the daily lives of people.
With this story, I have the wish to show the daily life of Littletato, what her life is like, and how incredible it is.
I love this story so much, and I'm happy to write it and to have created it.

Littletato was a girl that lived alone, she was always traveling through cities, looking for a good city to live in.
She loved to travel, experience new things, places, and nature, smell new smells, and hear new sounds.
Littletato was nineteen years old in 2019, and was born on February 4, 2000.
The girl stopped by a city called "San Francisco" and started analyzing, the weather, traffic, and people.
She found another girl while walking in San Francisco, it was afternoon, after mid-day, and a little cold.
Her name was Julia and she was eighteen years old, she was born on Jun 25, 2000.
They were in a cafeteria drinking a decaf coffee, sitting on a table outside the cafeteria.
The weather was cold, with wind, and a cloudy sky.
The two girls were wearing winter clothing, very warm and comfortable.
During the talk, they noticed that they had a lot in common.
Julia also liked to travel, to analyze the weather, people, and scenery of the cities.
"Do you like reading stories?" asked Littletato, who took a sip of her coffee.
"Yes, I love it, what about you Littletato?" asked Julia, looking at her, while holding her coffee mug.
"Me too, it's so good to meet someone that likes the same things as you right?" asked Littletato, happy.
"I agree, hehe," replied Julia, smiling, tucking her hair behind her ear.
"Where do you read stories?" asked Littletato, curious.
"I rent books from the city library, and sometimes I read some digital stories on the Wattpad website," replied Julia.
"Oh, how interesting, me too, I didn't know you used Wattpad too, hehe," said Littletato.
Julia said she lived alone in a rented house in the city.
Littletato said she was going for a walk around town, got up, and paid the bill for Julia.
Then Julia gave her number to Littletato, so they could talk again.
Littletato said that she was a traveler girl and that maybe would not stay in San Francisco, because she was only analyzing the city.
Julia was a little sad about that, she liked Littletato and found her an interesting girl.
The two said goodbye to each other with a hug, then Littletato walked to a bus stop and waited.

Littletato got a bus and started walking through the city.
She was thinking about Julia, about her eyes, her hair, and her gentle voice.
She listened to the music of the Folk genre on her phone, using earbuds, while looking out the bus window, thinking, and reflecting.
Littletato thought she was in love, just thinking about Julia's voice made her smile.
She was thinking about the city and Julia, while she looked at the city scenery.
The girl got up and pulled the bus rope, it stopped at a bus stop and the girl got off.
She started walking around the city, with her phone, wallet, money, and other useful things inside her backpack.
The girl remembered that she liked to program sometimes, to make computer programs and applications to help her be more efficient and faster.
Littletato created computer programs in her parent's house when she was a kid, she was fascinated by technology when she was younger.
She thought she would like to work on a programming job, and that it would be fun.
Then the girl started looking for programming jobs in San Francisco on the Internet.
She found some vacancies and sent her digital resume to several of them, she knew a lot of job websites.
A company accepted her resume and contacted her to give information about the job interview, place, and time.
Littletato ate a delicious dinner at a restaurant, and spent the night in a hotel, paying for accommodation.
She also took pictures of the city of San Francisco, of her dinner, and of the outside of the restaurant.
The girl liked to take pictures of good moments of her life, to keep as memories.
She sent those photos to a WhatsApp group called "Status", and also posted them on her WhatsApp status.
("WhatsApp" is an app that you can install on your smartphone, it lets you chat with people, but you need a phone number and a SIM card to use it.)

In the morning, she woke up, did her morning needs, and got a bus to the place of the interview.
It was a company called "Interworks Technologies", she entered the building and someone received her.
Then Littletato went through the interview, answering the questions of the interviewer.
After the interview ended, they said they would further review Littletato's resume and give her an answer later this week.
Some time passed, and it was already night, she came back to the hotel and grabbed her phone, looking at Julia's number, on WhatsApp.
She sent a message to her via VegesApp, saying:
"Hey Julia, it's me, Littletato, I was thinking bout' staying here in San Francisco... It seems to be a good city to live in.
I went through a job interview today, I think I'll get it... I'm very confident in this position."

Julia replied some minutes later:
"Oh, really?!... I'm so happy because of it :3
Good luck! I hope you get the job Littletato ^^"
"Thanks, Julia, happy because I'm gonna stay? :3" asked Littletato, happy.
"Yes, I think you're cool, and I like you... As a friend...
Do you consider me your friend?" asked Julia, curious.
"Yes Julia, and thanks, I think you're cool too ^^
Can I call you Ju?" asked Littletato.
"Hehe, yes you can, and can I call you Tato?" asked Julia, happy because Littletato would stay in the city.
"Yes you can Ju, hehe," replied Littletato.
"Okay, well, I'm gonna sleep now Tato, good night, sleep tight ^^," said Julia.
"Good night Ju, see you tomorrow :3," said Littletato.
Then Littletato slept on a peaceful night in San Francisco, very comfortable in her bed.

When she woke up in the morning, noticed that she had received a message on her phone.
She unlocked her screen to check it, it was from the company that had interviewed her, and she was accepted on the job.
In the message, there was more information about the job, hours, salary, holidays, days off, and other important information.
Littletato was so happy, she was smiling a lot, and sent a message to Julia to let her know the news.
"Hey Ju, I got the job, they accepted me! :3" said her.
"Really?! That's really great!
I knew you could do it, congrats Tato!" replied Julia.
"Thanks, hehe," said Littletato.
Littletato started working at the company, making computer programs and applications.
And also helped her co-workers, who were newbies, and were starting at the company.
She started living in a rented house.

Then, three months passed, and Littletato was already used to her new, stable life, in San Francisco.
Her relationship with Julia continued to grow stronger and stronger, and the two grew closer.
Littletato was in her house, she already worked today, and it was six in the afternoon.
She picked up her phone and opened the WhatsApp app.
Then she started typing a message to Julia, that said:
"Hey Ju, I have something to tell you :3
But can I ask you something first?"
"Yes, what's up Tato? :3" asked Julia.
"Can we meet at that cafeteria where we met for the first time?" asked Littletato.
"Okay, I'll go prepare myself, when are you going to be there?" asked Julia.
"At six and a half in the afternoon," replied Littletato.
"Okay, I'll be there, hihi," said Julia.

Then Littletato started to get ready to go to the cafeteria, left her house, and took a bus to go there.
They both got there, sat down, and ordered two decaf coffees, just like the first time they'd met.
"So... What do you want to tell me Tato?" asked Julia, while looking into Littletato's eyes.
"I... I like you, Ju... More than a friend...
You're so gentle with me and helped me a lot.
I think your hair is cute, and your voice too, you're so beautiful..." replied Littletato, a little shy and insecure.
"Hum... Thanks, Tato... I like you too...
I like the fact that I have a lot of things in common with you," said Julia, smiling, blushing, as she looked at Littletato.
Littletato picked up her chair and sat at the side of Julia, she hugged her and said "I love you," Julia said the same.
They looked at each other's lips, their heads started to approach and Littletato gave her a peck.
Littletato and Julia started kissing deeply, hugging tight, feeling happy and in love.

After some time, Littletato stopped the kiss for shortness of breath.
She looked into Julia's eyes, in love with her, and happy.
Littletato asked if Julia wanted to live with her and share the rent.
Julia said yes, and they moved to the house where Littletato lived.
The house was very good, it had planned furniture and a good bathroom.
Air conditioning, a heater, an electronic garage, and hot water.
Julia did not work, she said that she had some money stored in her bank account, and she paid her old rent without any problems.
Littletato said that she was going to work to pay her part of the rent and gather money to buy the house.
And also do some investments in fixed and variable income, stock exchange, cryptocurrencies, and other investments.

---

A few months had passed, and Littletato had worked hard, gathering money in her bank account, as well as making safe investments.
She managed to buy the house of the owner for her and Julia to live, without having to pay rent, only paying the energy and water bills and the house taxes.
Then Littletato and Julia started living there, eating, drinking, cleaning the house, and having fun together.
Julia said she was very happy, living together with Littletato, her girlfriend.
Littletato arrived home from her job, it was afternoon, already getting dark, she entered the house and locked the front door, saying "I'm home love".
Julia was sitting on the couch in the living room, watching a series on Netflix, "Welcome back honey," said she.
Littletato sat by her side and hugged her tight, kissing her lips.
Julia prepared dinner with the help of Littletato, and the two ate while talking a little, after that, they watched something on Netflix for some minutes.

Then, they went to the bedroom and lay down on the bed, covering themselves with the blanket.
Littletato hugged Julia tightly from behind and kissed her neck, Julia shivered and closed her eyes, feeling sleepy.
"I love you, Tato," said Julia, smiling, and kissed Littletato's hand.
"I love you too, Ju," said Littletato, who sniffed Julia's hair and closed her eyes.
They slept soundly into the night, waiting for tomorrow, for a new day they would spend together.

You are reading: The Life of Littletato
Chapter: 2 - The Beginning, Part Two






Littletato was coming back home, she finished her work and was carrying a bag of food that she brought from the market.
She found a friend of hers, Littletato made that friend while she was traveling through San Francisco, they met on the bus.
Her friend was a sweet potato called Yam, he was a man.
"Hi Yam, good to see you!" said Littletato looking at Yam.
"Good to see you too, Tato," replied Yam while smiling.
They talked for some time.
"Hey Tato, did you know that in Las Vegas they sell meat and vegetable even if there are cows in there?" asked Yam.
"I didn't know, it is very bad," said Littletato.
"Yeah, I agree," replied Yam, while looking a bit sad.
"Well, I gotta go, my sister is in town again, I brought her favorite chocolates.
I gotta go back home, or else she will be angry at me, hehe, see you later Tato," said Yam, who started walking back home, waving goodbye to Littletato.
"Bye, see you later Yam," replied Littletato, waving goodbye back.

Littletato arrived back home, she talked to Julia about the conversation that she had with Yam.
Julia said that she wanted to meet Yam sometime soon, Littletato said she is going to introduce Yam to her.
Littletato placed the food bag on top of the table and helped Julia prepare the dinner.
They ate dinner together while talking a little.
Julia asked Littletato how her was her job today.
Littletato said that it was pretty cool, she met a new coworker who started working on the company.
Her name was Mia, she was a carrot, Littletato helped her with a problem she had with the program she was making.
Then Julia and Littletato finished eating, they made their necessities, and walked to the bedroom.
The couple lied on the bed and covered themselves with the blanket.
Littletato hugged Julia tight because it was cold, they slept.

On the other day, Littletato woke up but Julia did not.
She looked at the clock and saw that it was five in the morning.
Littletato got out of bed and walked to the bathroom to make her morning necessities.
After that, she walked to the kitchen and started making breakfast.
She picked up two mugs and poured milk and chocolate powder on them, mixing the chocolate powder and milk, with the help of a spoon.
Then she picked up two plates and placed two slices of bread on each one.
She grabbed a knife and butter, passing butter on all of the slices of bread.
Then she came back to the bedroom and woke up Julia.
Julia walked to the bathroom to do her morning necessities.

Both walked to the kitchen and ate breakfast together.
"You still have some time before going to work, right honey?" asked Julia.
"Yes, why the question my dear?" asked Littletato.
"It's because I miss you when you go to work, honey," said Julia, looking a little sad.
Littletato sat at the side of Julia and hugged her tight, giving a kiss on her lips.
"It's okay, honey, when I get back home, I'll be all yours okay?" asked Littletato.
"Okay, hehe, I love you my lil potato," said Julia, looking passionately at Littletato.
Both of them finished eating, Julia thought it was very delicious, Littletato too.

Then Littletato gave a kiss on the lips of Julia and got up, walking to the living room.
She had a computer in her house, she walked close to it and sat on the chair, turning the computer on.
Julia walked to the bedroom and wore a hoodie, it was a little cold.
Julia had a laptop, she walked to the living room and grabbed it, putting her laptop on the side of Littletato's computer.
She turned it on and started using it, opening the browser to browse the Internet.
After some time using the browser, Julia opened the game Countable Vegetrike 1.6 to play a little.
This game was an FPS or first-person shooter game where you needed to complete an objective.
Littletato looked to her right and noticed Julia there, she smiled, then opened the Vegebook website, and logged in to her account.
(Vegebook is a website where you can talk to a lot of people and can have a profile, a lot of people use it only to talk and keep in contact with their family.)
She looked at the chat, seeing her friends online.
Even if those friends were just digital friends, she was happy to have them.
And she could count on them because they would help her.
Littletato began to roll the page down.
Her friends always posted some news, one news got her attention.
It was news talking about how New York citizens were trying to fight the fruits and wanting freedom.
The news said that the fruits were invading New York and the vegetables did not like that.
Littletato thought that San Francisco was good because of that.
The city of San Francisco was stabilized, with no fight between the citizens.

Then Littletato closed the page and started rolling her Vegebook feed again.
Her old friend Yam sent a message to her in Vegebook.
She clicked on the message to see what it was.
Yam said that in New York there were good jobs, that it was a good city to live in.
Littletato replied that she already had a job in San Francisco, and had bought a house too.
She also said that she was living with her girlfriend.
Yam said that it was good and that he was happy for Littletato, he wished happiness for the couple.
Littletato sent a smile emoji and said thanks.
"And you Yam, have a girlfriend?" asked Littletato.
"No, I'm single, hehe, I'm focusing more on my job, and finishing my college," said Yam.
"Oh, what college are you doing?" asked Littletato.
"It's mechanical engineering," replied Yam.
"That sounds very cool, good luck on it!" said Littletato.
"Thanks, Tato ^^," said Yam.
She said that she was going to work, and said goodbye to Yam, he wished her luck and said goodbye back.
Littletato closed the Vegebook website and turned off her computer, then she prepared herself to go to work.
Then the girl walked to the living room's door, the match of Julia had finished, she got off her chair and walked to where Littletato was.
Julia hugged Littletato tight and kissed her lips, "Good luck honey, good work," said Julia, smiling.
"Thanks, honey," said Littletato, kissing Julia's lips back.
Then Littletato started to walk to her job, she arrived there and started working on her technology and programming job.

After some hours of working, it was six PM, Littletato got all of her stuff and left the company building, she started walking home.
Julia was watching a game Livestream on Vegetube with her feet on the computer's table, she was eating a chocolate stuffed biscuit.
Littletato arrived home and opened the door, she locked the door and gave a kiss on Julia's lips.
"Welcome home honey," said Julia, smiling and looking at her.
"Thanks, hon," replied Littletato, who walked to the bedroom and changed herself.
Then Littletato made something for her and Julia to eat, she brought Julia's plate to her, and left it on top of Julia's computer table, close to her laptop.
After that, Littletato ate and drank a little water, then she sat on her computer's chair and turned her computer on.
The girl waited for the computer to turn on and opened the Mozilla Firefox web browser.
After that, she opened the Vegetube website to search for a rock song, she searched for one and chose it, putting it to play.
Littletato looked to her right and saw Julia, she hugged Julia tight and kissed her lips, saying "I love you".
Julia said I love you back and kissed Littletato's lips.
Then Julia closed the game Livestream, she opened the game Countable Vegetrike 1.6 to play again.
The girl was in the terrorist team, she needed to plant a bomb, the Counter-terrorist team needed to defuse it.
Julia was very good at it, she had made many kills and headshots.

Littletato asked if she could play with her.
Julia said yes and sent the IP of the server she was playing to the Vegesapp of Littletato, Julia used the Vegesapp Web website to send the IP of the server to Littletato.
Littletato then opened Vegesapp on the browser of her computer to get the IP, also using Vegesapp Web.
(Vegesapp is an app that you can install on your smartphone, it lets you chat with people, you need a phone number and a sim card to use it.)
She opened the FPS game, came back to the browser, and copied the IP.
Then opened the game again and pasted the IP.
She started playing the game and was on the same team as Julia.
Julia was on her right, playing on her laptop.
When Julia died, Littletato could see where the enemy was, by looking at Julia's screen.
Littletato and Julia had made many kills together, they were happy by playing the game.

The couple was a little tired, they turned off their devices and Julia left her laptop charging.
It was eleven at night, Littletato started preparing dinner with Julia.
They ate together and waited a little to sleep, they drank some water too.
Littletato and Julia locked the front door and turned off the lights.
The girl held Julia in her arms, walking with her to the bedroom.
Then she left Julia laid on the bed and laid beside her, covering herself and Julia with the blanket.
She kissed Julia's lips and hugged her tight, sleeping with her, dreaming good dreams.

You are reading: The Life of Littletato
Chapter: 3 - The Work






Littletato woke up at six in the morning, looking at the sun hitting the bedroom's window crack, which was closed.
She was a little tired, so she hugged Julia and slept again.

After some time sleeping, the clock ringed and Littletato woke up.
She looked at the time, it was eleven in the morning.
She got out of bed and walked to the bathroom to do her morning necessities.
After that, Littletato walked to the kitchen to prepare breakfast.
Littletato prepared coffee with milk for her and Julia, leaving the two mugs on top of the table.
She prepared some slices of bread with butter too.

Then Littletato walked to the bedroom and kissed Julia's cheeks, saying:
"Good morning, honey."

Julia slowly opened her eyes and looked at Littletato.
Littletato laid beside Julia and kissed her lips.
Julia smiled while looking at Littletato, hugging her tight.
Littletato hugged back and caressed Julia's hair, telling her that breakfast was ready.

Julia walked to the bathroom to do her morning needs.
She brushed her teeth, used some floss, and combed her hair.
Then she walked to the kitchen, Littletato walked there with her.
They both sat at the table and started eating.
Julia and Littletato loved the taste of coffee in the morning.
Julia looked at Littletato and said that she was going to call her sister to come by for a visit.
Littletato said that she wished to meet Julia's sister, smiling.
Julia smiled back and said:
"I'm glad that you want to meet her, honey, hehe, thanks," said Julia.
"Hehe, no problem hon," replied Littletato.

Then Littletato finished eating and got up, going to the bedroom to prepare herself to work.
Julia grabbed her phone and sent a message to her sister, asking if she would like to visit Julia's house.
Her sister replied positively, saying that she was going to arrive there at six and a half in the afternoon.
Julia walked to the bedroom and kissed Littletato's cheek, smiling.
Littletato kissed Julia back and finished preparing herself to work.
She grabbed her backpack and her phone, then walked to the living room's door.
Littletato said that she was going to get back home at six in the afternoon.
Julia said that her sister was going to arrive at six and a half in the afternoon.
Then Littletato smiled and said goodbye to Julia, kissing her lips.
Julia said goodbye back, smiling and waving her hand, then she locked the door of the house.

Littletato started walking to her work while listening to some songs on her phone.
She arrived at the building where she worked, she walked inside it and arrived at her desk.
Littletato sat at her chair and turned on her computer.
Her coworker Mia was on the desk at the left of Littletato.
After turning her computer on, she opened a code editor and started fixing the errors of an app.
Littletato sometimes was asked to fix smartphones at work, she knew how to fix them.
While Littletato was working, Julia was preparing the house for her sister's visit, cleaning, and organizing it.
Her sister was called Vitória, she was nineteen years old, Julia had eighteen.

Littletato programmed more and more, fixing all the errors on the app.
Mia said that she needed some help, and Littletato helped her.
Mia was not understanding how she was supposed to do a part of the app that her boss told her.
So Littletato explained that to her and gave a few examples too, showing these examples on the screen of Littletato's computer.
After that, Mia said thanks and smiled at Littletato, then she continued doing her job.
Littletato continued programming, she tested the app to see if the errors still happened.
They did not happen again, she started working on the visual part of another app.

Hours passed and Littletato finished her job, she got out of the building and started walking.
She was walking back home while listening to some songs on her phone.
Then she noticed some televisions on a shop window, Littletato paused the music and listened to the TV.
It said that a war was happening in Las Vegas and the vegetables were fighting against some animals that were invading the city.
Littletato became a little sad to know that, she picked up her phone and opened the gallery app.
She looked at a picture of her and Julia hugging tight, smiling.
Littletato smiled and became a little happier, forgetting about the war in Las Vegas.
She looked at the time and saw that it was almost six and a half in the afternoon.
Littletato turned off the phone screen and started walking back home again.
The girl arrived there and opened the front door.
She kissed Julia's lips and hugged her, after that, she walked to the bedroom and changed herself.
They both walked to the living room and waited for Vitória to come by.

After some time waiting, Vitória arrived.
Littletato said hello to Vitória and she said hello back.
Julia said that Littletato was her girlfriend, and Vitória was happy to know that.
Vitória hugged Julia tight and said: "I missed you so much, sis!"
"I missed you too, sis," replied Julia.
Then Vitória walked close to Littletato and shook her hand.

Chapter: 4 - The Visit of Vitória, the Relaxing Anime






Vitória said that there were great jobs in the city that she lived.

This city is great," replied Julia.

Julia walked to the kitchen and started making the afternoon coffee.
Then Littletato and Vitória walked to the kitchen, the trio started to eat while talking.
"So, how is your job, Littletato?" asked Vitória.

"Well, I work in a technology company, I make apps, programs, and fix smartphones sometimes.
It is great, programming has been a great passion for me.
I'm so happy, hehe," replied Littletato while smiling, looking at Vitória.

Chapter: 5 - The Space Traveler Dream






Littletato was drawing something on her computer using a program called Paint Tool SAI.
It was a program where you could draw digitally, using pencils, brushes, and make line art.
She liked to use that program to draw stuff, she finished drawing a potato some days ago.
Littletato was drawing an anime girl today, the girl had yellow hair and blue eyes.
She was drawing the girl while listening to some songs of the Future Bounce genre on Vegetube.
Julia was in the bedroom using her laptop, talking with some friends on Vegebook and Vegewitter.
Littletato was a little hungry and asked if Julia wanted to make dinner with her.
Julia said yes and they both walked to the kitchen, they prepared rice with beans and some salad to eat.
They ate together while talking a little, looking at each other, and smiling.
"Hey, honey, what you were drawing there?" asked Julia, looking at the screen of Littletato's computer.
"It's just an idea that I had, of an anime girl with an orange cat on her lap, what do you think sweetie?" asked Littletato.
"I think it is very good honey, you're so good at drawing, I wanted to know how to draw as well as you," replied Julia.
"Hehe, thanks honey, I'm happy that you think that, I would love to teach you how to draw someday," said Littletato.

Then they finished eating, they cleaned up the table and Littletato helped Julia wash the dishes.
They both walked to the living room, Littletato turned on her computer and opened the Paint Tool SAI program.
Julia sat beside her, looking at the screen, Littletato opened the file of the drawing of the anime girl with an orange cat.
Littletato started teaching Julia how to draw, she hid the line art of the drawing to show Julia how to draw the line art.
She drew and looked at Julia, giving the mouse for her to try, Julia started drawing the line art, clicking with the mouse.
Julia was very good at it, she knew how to draw very easily, Littletato smiled while looking at her, being proud.
Julia started drawing cats, stars, cars, Littletato was surprised, she was very happy that Julia could draw so well.
"Hey honey, maybe you should download Paint Tool SAI on your computer, you're very good at drawing!" said Littletato.
"Yes, I agree, can you send me the link so I can download it?" asked Julia.
"Yes honey," said Littletato, then she sent the download link of the program to Julia through Vegesapp Web.
Julia opened her laptop and turned it on, opening Mozilla Vegefox and opening the link, putting the program to download.
Julia said she was a little tired, Littletato said that too, they both turned off their devices and gone to the bedroom.
They laid on the bed and covered themselves with the blanket, hugging tight and sleeping well.

Julia and Littletato started dreaming together, they were on a cold planet, a blue planet.
Julia was shivering, hugging herself, and sighing, she wanted to find somewhere warm to stay.
She looked around and did not know the environment, she was not used to alien things.
She was in doubt about the animals and life on that planet, she was curious and wanted to learn more and more about the place.
There was a strange creature close to them, it had a human shape, his head was a screen, they did not understand what it said.
Looks like it was speaking an alien language, it was looking a little surprised and also happy, like he never saw humans before.
The couple could understand his language a little bit, he said that he was called Spet.
He stopped looking at them and walked to his house, entering it and closing the door.
Julia and Littletato started walking around the planet, looking at some strange animals.
They noticed that they had a multi-tool, it could mine gems and ores, it could also manipulate the terrain and fight aliens.
The couple also had a jetpack or jump pack, with which they could jump and climb stuff.
Julia started walking close to a red plant and collected it with her hands, she received the oxygen element.
They had an Exo suit, it was like a backpack where they could store things and technologies, it also helped them stay alive.
Julia opened the inventory of her Exo suit and saw that she had the oxygen element on her inventory.
She had a device in her Exo suit called Life Support, it helped them to stay alive, she used her oxygen to refuel the device.
Littletato did that too, they thought that the planet they were on was very weird.
They both started walking close to a spaceship, it recognized them like it was their spaceship.
The couple jumped on top of the spaceship and the door of it opened, they entered it and sat.

Littletato did not know how to drive the spaceship, so she pulled a switch that was in the same position where the keys were in cars.
The spaceship turned on, they heard a laser sound, a sound of something alien being activated.
Littletato pushed a button, the spaceship took off and began to hover in the air, they were a little scared by that.
Littletato grabbed the steering wheel of the spaceship and moved it to the right, turning the spaceship in 360º.
"Are you sure that you know how to drive this spaceship honey?" asked Julia which was behind Littletato.
"No honey, I'm just trying to learn how to drive it," said Littletato.
The beak of the spaceship was pointing at an animal on the planet, Littletato pressed a button which she did not know what did.
A laser was shot at the animal, it died, that laser came from the spaceship, it was used to mine asteroids in space.
"Oops," said Littletato with a worried face, looking at the animal.
Then a Sentinel appeared close to the spaceship, scanning them, it looks like they committed a space crime and had a wanted level there.
Littletato stepped on the accelerator of the spaceship and began to fly around, trying to escape the sentinel, which was like a planetary policeman.
She wanted to leave the planet to escape and pointed the beak of the spaceship up.
The spaceship passed through the atmosphere and the couple arrived in space.
Littletato thought that it was beautiful out there, with a lot of planets, space, and the sun of that galaxy.

The galaxy was called Rameses B, Littletato could upload the info of the galaxy and gain units, which were like space money.
Littletato stepped on the accelerator of the spaceship and began flying around the galaxy.
She saw an asteroid and pushed the same button that killed the animal, the spaceship fired its laser and mined the asteroid.
The spaceship collected the elements from the asteroid, which was silver, it could be used to build heat and toxic protections.
"This game is very fun!" said Littletato, excited when firing the laser.
"Wait... are we in a game?" asked Julia in doubt.
"Uh... I guess so, this looks like a game that I saw some months ago, so I thought this was that game," said Littletato.
"Weird... hey honey, can we go to another planet?" asked Julia.
"Of course honey, what type of planet do you want?" asked Littletato.
"A very hot one, I was beginning to freeze at the planet we were before," said Julia.
"Okay hon," said Littletato, which started to drive the spaceship, looking for a warm planet.
She found one and began entering its atmosphere, the window of the spaceship was a little warm because of the atmospheric pressure.

Littletato parked the spaceship close to a planet base and came out of the spaceship along with Julia.
They started walking around the planet looking for something to do.
The Life Support device of Littletato was a little empty, she collected some oxygen with her hands, and refilled it.
Julia did that too, she also recharged her Hazard Protection device with Sodium.
That device was used to continually monitor and stabilize the user's environment, protecting the user from heat, cold, toxicity, or radiation.
Littletato started looking at a crashed spaceship, there was a terminal close to it.
She started reading the log of the machine, it looked like some space pirates shot this spaceship, trying to steal a rare plant that it had.
Littletato discovered that the pilot of the spaceship escaped by running around this planet.
The pilot also found a deposit of very rare materials, some elements used to recharge protection devices, and some materials to build upgrades.
Littletato could see the location of the deposit on her radar, she asked Julia if the wanted to go there.
Julia said yes, after that, she looked at a small animal that was close to them, it looked very cute.
Julia tried to give food to it and it ate the food, it began to follow Julia.
"Ah, honey, it is so cute, can we bring it with us?" asked Julia smiling at the animal.
"Of course honey, hehe," said Littletato smiling.
Then Julia grabbed the animal and began to follow Littletato.
Littletato grabbed some materials that were closed to the crashed spaceship and walked to her spaceship.
Julia and she entered the spaceship, Littletato turned the spaceship on, taking off and driving to the deposit.
Then the dream changed to another dream, Littletato and Julia were sleeping happy, together, in love with each other.

"Okay hon, let's go there," says Littletato.

Then they walk to the marketplace to buy food, Littletato buys bread, rice and beans, and a bottle of Coca-Cola.

Chapter: 12 - The Cookie, Cyberpunk, and the Castle of Glass Dreams






It was a Friday, Littletato was dreaming of cookies, she ate a lot of them.
She asked herself why she always had food dreams, maybe it is because she loved eating stuff.
Littletato was eating cookies, she was sat on a throne, looking at a pile of gold.
She thought that she was a queen or a princess, some royal person.
There was a giant pile of cookies in front of her, she could eat every cookie.
Littletato was wearing a wool coat, it was a stylish thing to wear.
She was known as "The queen of eating" or "The queen of the cookies" because she ate and produced a lot of cookies.
Littletato could press a button and it would make cookies for her.
There were also grandmothers, farms, mines, factories, and portals that produced cookies for her.
Her cookie factory was known everywhere in the world, she was very famous for making cookies.
The TV news was flooded with the news about her and her cookie factory, she was a very good cookie maker.
After some years, cookies became the new currency and people threw the old paper money away.

Then another dream came in, Littletato was driving on a highway with a car that had some purple neon on its sides.
The car's radio was playing a track of the Synth wave genre, Littletato liked to feel the wind on her hair, she liked to listen to the song while driving on the highway.
There were a lot of people on the highway too, driving their cars, Littletato looked at her car and thought that it was a Delorean.
A fast car passed by her, it was a car with red neon on its sides, it looked like a car from a rebel group that tried to fight for freedom in the city where Littletato was.
That group fought for freedom and freedom of speech, they did not agree with the city's governor's choice of monitoring the population.
Littletato stepped on the car's accelerator and came face to face with the person inside the red neon car.
The person lowered the car window, it was a girl that had red LEDs on her hair, she looked punk, and had purple eye makeup on her eyes.
"Hey, you're new here, right? Wanna join our group?" asked the girl.
"What your group is about?" asked Littletato.
"We fight for freedom and fight to deactivate the surveillance system that exists in the city, the governor created it to monitor people's life.
We don't want that, we want freedom and privacy, we have good hackers on our side," said her.
"Oh, that sounds cool, what is your name?" asked Littletato while driving fast, following the red neon car.
"My name is Mika, what's yours?" asked the red LED girl.
"Littletato, nice to meet you Mika," said Littletato.
"Nice to meet you too, Littletato," said Mika, smiling.
Then Littletato drove together with Mika, they arrived at the headquarters of "The Underdogs", the rebel group of Mika.

After that, the dream switched to another dream, Littletato was feeling very calm inside that dream, she felt happy and relaxed.
She was seeing a beautiful castle of glass, it was transparent and you could see the things inside it, it was really beautiful.
Behind the castle of glass was a wonderful blue sky and some white clouds, it was like Littletato was high in the sky, close to the clouds.
Littletato could look at the sun and see it paint the clouds yellow, see it pass through the clouds.
The castle of glass was empty, but Littletato did not felt lonely or sad, she was happy for being in such a good and relaxing place.
It was like the castle was traveling on top of the clouds, that the clouds were holding it.
Littletato could fly in the sky even if she had no wings, she began flying close to the castle and landed close to its door.
Its door was big and tall, Littletato pushed the door and it opened, she started walking inside the castle.
The castle of glass had various beautiful chandeliers with a lot of colorful jewels hanging on them.
Littletato thought that it was very beautiful, seeing all those amazing chandeliers with red, pink, purple, white, black, blue, green, yellow, and grey jewels hanging on them.
She could see the sunlight coming inside the castle of glass and forming a rainbow inside it.
Her eyes shone with amazement and astonishment, Littletato was in a very beautiful place.
The castle of glass was really big, she began walking inside it and opening all of its doors, she saw a library, a room with a bed and a wardrobe.
And a dining room with a really wide table, the table was filled with slices of lemon cake on the plates and had bottles of Coca-cola close to a big cake that was on the end of the table.
Littletato thought that there was a party going on there, even if there was no one nearby, she sat at a chair.

Suddenly, a purple alicorn pony appeared there in the dining room, she said that her name was Twilight Sparkle, and was surprised to see a human for the first time.
(There goes me again inserting "My Little Pony: Friendship Is Magic" in my stories xD.
I love MLP: FIM, I can't help but put it in other things I love, which are my stories :3.)
"Hello there, where do you come from?" asked Twilight Sparkle while looking at Littletato.
Littletato was surprised at the sight of the little pony, she never saw a pony or an alicorn before, she looked at her wings and her horn.
"Some minutes ago I just realized that I was floating in the sky close to a castle of glass, I could fly, so I began flying towards that castle.
And I began exploring this castle and opening its doors, the chandeliers here are so beautiful.
I already love this place even if I haven't spent much time in here," said Littletato while looking at the ceiling of the castle.
"Oh, that's interesting, this castle floats high in the sky, so it is really hard for people to visit it or even know that it is real.
So I don't know how you got in here, but... You can stay here if you want... By the way, what is your name?" asked Twilight Sparkle.
"My name is Littletato, what is yours?" asked Littletato smiling lightly while looking at Twilight.
"My name is Twilight Sparkle, so, you can fly right?" asked Twilight.
"Yeah, I guess, can I show you?" asked Littletato, getting up from the chair.
"Yes, please," said Twilight Sparkle.

Then Littletato began floating towards the ceiling of the dining room like she was floating on the water.
Twilight Sparkle was surprised by that, she used her magic to get Littletato on the floor again, her horn shone in purple.
"My friends are gonna come here for a birthday party, do you wanna join us Littletato?" asked Twilight Sparkle, smiling at Littletato.
"Of course!" said Littletato smiling, "Whose birthday is it?" asked her.
"It's Dashie's birthday, Rainbow Dash, my friend," said Twilight Sparkle.
"Oh, can she create rainbows?" asked Littletato with her eyes shining with amazement.
"Well... Yeah, I guess, when she flies fast she creates a sonic rainbow which is kind of like flying faster than the speed of light, then a rainbow appears behind her," said Twilight Sparkle.
"Wow, that's awesome," said Littletato putting her hands on her cheeks and smiling.
"That's what she would say if she saw something awesome," said Twilight Sparkle while giggling a little.
"So, I'm gonna read a book for thirty minutes to wait for my friends to arrive here okay?" asked Twilight Sparkle.
"Okay, can I sleep in here?" asked Littletato while looking at Twilight Sparkle.
"Of course, hehe, I think you're a good person.
In fact, the first time I saw you here today I thought you were an alien," said Twilight Sparkle while giggling a little.
"But I read in a book about the legend of the humans, creatures that were bipeds, creatures that walked on two legs and held things with their hands.
So I was not so surprised of seeing you, I thought 'Oh, I finally saw a human in my life, they say that they are rare'," said Twilight Sparkle while smiling and looking at Littletato.

"Come with me, I'm gonna show you your room, I always have a free room for guests," said Twilight Sparkle who began trotting to the stairs.
Littletato followed her and they arrived at a door, Twilight opened the door and Littletato saw a room with a bed, wardrobe, and a writing desk.
The girl entered the room and began walking inside it to familiarize herself with the room.
"This is your room, have fun," said Twilight while smiling.
"Oh, and another thing, the castle is not made of glass, it's just a spell that I use to keep ponies away from here and prevent pegasus from hitting the castle accidentally," said Twilight, who made her horn glow and turned on the colors of the castle.
The castle was now opaque and you could see that it was made of crystals, Twilight Sparkle said to Littletato that a crystal tree was planted on the ground down there.
Twilight Sparkle said that the tree grew and generated a crystal castle, that castle began flying and stopped flying when it reached the sky.
And now they have a beautiful crystal castle to live inside and house all of their friends and stuff.

Spike, the purple baby dragon assistant, and friend of Twilight Sparkle arrived, he walked upstairs while looking for Twilight.
"Twilight? Twilight? Where are you?" asked him.
"I'm up here Spike, at the guest's room," said Twilight Sparkle.
Then Spike walked there and saw Littletato.
"Who is she?" asked Spike.
"She is my new friend, Littletato, she said that she just appeared close to the castle and she thought that it was a castle of glass.
Then she began exploring the castle and looking at it, she is gonna stay here with us Spike," said Twilight Sparkle smiling.
"Oh, okay, nice to meet you, Littletato," said Spike, walking close to Littletato and shaking her hand.
Littletato shook the hand of Spike back and smiled, "Nice to meet you too, Spike".
"Okay, I'm gonna read my comic book Twilight, tell me when the others arrive," said Spike, going downstairs and walking inside the library.
"Okay Spike," said Twilight Sparkle before he left the room.
"I'll tell you too when the girls arrive okay?" asked Twilight Sparkle.
"Okay, thanks Twilight," said Littletato smiling.
"No problem, hehe," said Twilight Sparkle, who closed the door, trotted downstairs, and entered inside the library, getting a book with her horn magic and laying on the ground.

Littletato laid on her bed and looked at the ceiling, smiling happily while feeling her current feelings and thinking about where she is right now.
She thought that she was experiencing a lot of new things, new feelings.
Littletato met new people, she met a purple pony alicorn who had wings, a horn, and magic.
The girl closed her eyes, after some minutes she began sleeping, she woke up in yet another dream.
Littletato woke up and smiled while remembering and thinking about the dreams she had.
The dream about how she was a cookie producer and had a cookie company that dominated the world and made cookies the new currency.
That dream of Synthwave stuff and the rebel group of Mika.
And that awesome dream about the castle of glass that was not made of glass and there were a purple pony and a purple dragon inside and a birthday party was going to happen.
Littletato thought about those three dreams, she wondered how her mind could create those dreams even if she did not know those people and those places.
She thought that she was really traveling to those places when she dreamt, like astral projection.

Chapter: 13 - The Cupcake Dream and the Superhero Movie






It was a Friday, before midnight, Littletato was dreaming, she was very calm inside her current dream, she felt happy and relaxed.
She was seeing a beautiful castle of glass, it was transparent and you could see the things inside it, it was really beautiful.
Behind the castle of glass was a wonderful blue sky and some white clouds, it was like Littletato was high in the sky, close to the clouds.
Some minutes passed inside her dream, a lot of things happened, she was talking with an alicorn pony called Twilight Sparkle.
The castle was not made of glass, it was opaque and Twilight Sparkle could use her horn magic to change the castle between its two modes, glass and opaque.
Littletato met spike, the purple baby dragon assistant of Twilight Sparkle, he could spit fire through his mouth.
Julia was dreaming about a castle, she is sat on a very wide table, the part where she was sat had a big bowl of pink cupcakes.
The rest of the table was filled with a mixture of sweet and savory, pies, cakes, coxinha, pastry, and other foods.
She ate a cupcake, the taste of the cupcake reminded her of Pinkie Pie, a pink earth pony from My Little Pony who had a dark pink mane.
Then a bed fell from the ceiling and landed on the ground close to Julia.
She got up and laid on the bed, then Julia noticed that a small fridge was there, on the other side of the room.
Julia got up from the bed and walked close to the fridge, opening it and grabbing a can of Coca-cola.

The girl looked at the door, it was a tall door, it was made of wood, dark wood just like the walls.
The house looked like an old house from inside, a house of rich people.
There were two big windows on the right of Julia, she looked at them, they had beautiful white curtains.
There was a light outside of the windows, a bright white light that did not let Julia see past the windows.
Julia looked at the door again, the door opened, Pinkie Pie was behind the door, opening it.
Pinkie Pie flew around the dining room even if she could not fly, yelling "Weeeeeeeeeee!"
"Hi, I'm Pinkie Pie, and I threw this party just for you!" said Pinkie Pie, holding Julia's hands with her hoofs.
"Do you like the food?" asked Pinkie Pie, smiling.
"Yes, it is pretty good, I ate only one cupcake actually, I know you from a cartoon called My Little Pony," said Julia, smiling at her.
"You only ate one cupcake?!" asked Pinkie Pie yelling, surprised, "I don't know what is a 'cartoon', what is it?" asked Pinkie Pie, curious.
"Oh, it is... nothing, I know you from somewhere else than here, anyway, why you threw this party for me Pinkie Pie?" asked Julia.
"Because you're a good person, I know you, Julia, and you're a caring person and good friend to me, you always help me," said Pinkie Pie, hugging Julia tight.
"Oh, thanks Pinkie Pie, I'm really happy that you think that," said Julia, returning the hug while smiling.
"But... I never met Pinkie Pie, how she is my friend?" thought Julia, curious.
"Anyway, are you gonna eat the food?" asked Pinkie Pie, breaking out from the hug while looking at the table and looking back at Julia.
"Yes, do you wanna eat with me? I don't think I can handle all that food," asked Julia while giggling a little.
"Yes, hehe, yay!" said Pinkie Pie, jumping happily on top of a chair and starting to eat some pies.
Julia made the same, they started to eat together, the food was very delicious.

Then, after some time eating, Pinkie Pie and Julia finished eating all of the food.
"I'm gonna get some rest Julia, my tummy hurts from so much food," said Pinkie Pie with her hoof on her belly.
"If you need me I'm gonna be in my room upstairs okay?" said Pinkie Pie, starting to walking to the door, closing it, and walking upstairs.
"Okay Pinkie Pie," said Julia before Pinkie Pie left the dining room.
Then Julia walked to the small fridge, the letters "TPF" were written on the door of the fridge.
Julia grabbed a can of Coca-cola out of the fridge and started drinking it to relieve the pain in her tummy.
She finished drinking the can and threw it inside the trash can that was there.
After that, Julia laid on the bed looking at the beautiful chandelier that was on the ceiling.
She felt a little tired, Julia closed her eyes and started to sleep.

After some minutes, Julia still had her eyes closed, she heard a familiar voice calling her.
"Julia... wake up, wake up... Hey, Julia, wake up," said the voice.
Julia opened her eyes and everything was blurry, she started to see well again, she saw the same room with dark wood walls.
In front of her was Littletato, telling her to wake up, and that the breakfast is ready.
After that, she heard Littletato's voice more realistically.
Julia opened her eyes again, she woke up, it was not a dream anymore, her brain used the real voice of Littletato to create a dream.
After some seconds, Julia got up and hugged Littletato, Littletato kissed Julia's lips and smiled, it was a Saturday.
"I had a dream with Pinkie Pie, and after some minutes in that dream, I heard your voice call me to wake up cause breakfast was ready hon," said Julia.
"Oh, I think your brain used my voice as a dream 'fuel', my brain does that sometimes, it's good that I can wake you up more easily," said Littletato while giggling a little.
"Hehe, I love you hon," said Julia, kissing Littletato's lips.
"I love you too my little potato," said Littletato, kissing Julia's lips back.
Then Julia got up and walked to the bathroom, she started making her morning needs.

Then the couple walked to the kitchen and started to eat breakfast, Littletato had made eggs with bacon.
"Hey honey, today I dreamed about cookies, and a cookie factory, also about Twilight Sparkle and her crystal castle, it was very good," said Littletato while eating.
"Oh, that sounds interesting hon, I dreamed with Pinkie Pie today, she is my favorite character of My Little Pony," said Júlia smiling, remembering the dream.
"How was that dream hon?" asked Littletato, curious.
"I noticed that I was sitting on the chair of a wide table, it had a lot of pink cupcakes and other foods, sweet and savory.
Then I ate one cupcake, suddenly a bed fell from the ceiling and landed next to me, that was normal for me.
There was a fridge on the other side of the room, I got up and walked close to it, opening it and grabbing a can of Coca-cola.
Then Pinkie Pie appeared there and said that she made that party just for me, I was happy for her to be there, it was good to know her.
The food was too much, I invited her to eat with me, she accepted and we ate a lot, our tummies hurt.
Then I laid on the bed and slept, then I woke up in the dream and after that, in real life," explained Julia while looking at Littletato.
"Oh, that's very interesting honey, it was a really good dream," said Littletato, smiling.
"Yeah, hehe," said Julia.
Then the couple finished eating, they walked to the living room to watch a movie.
Littletato heard that a new movie was out on the Vegeflix app, the couple sat on the couch and Littletato turned on the Smart TV.
After that, Littletato searched for the movie "The Vegengers: Infinite Vegetablewar" at Vegeflix.
"My sister said that this movie is very good," said Julia, looking at Littletato.
"Oh, let's watch it then hon, do you want to post a picture of us and the movie on the Vegesapp status?" asked Littletato.
"Yes, let's do it hon," said Julia smiling.

Then Littletato pressed play on the movie and grabbed her smartphone, she paused the movie and took a selfie of her, Julia, and the TV.
Littletato posted that picture on her Vegesapp status, she sent the photo to Julia so she could post it on her status too.
Julia posted the photo on her status, Vitória sent her a message on Vegesapp, she said that she is having fun with her boyfriend in New York.
After that, Julia replied to Vitória with some happy face emojis, Vitória said "Good movie sis!" to Julia.
"Thanks, sis! ^^" replied Julia, Julia said that she is having fun with Littletato.
Vitória said that she is happy for Julia, Julia is also happy for her sister.
Littletato asked who it was, Julia said it was her sister, saying that Vitória was having fun with her boyfriend in New York.
Then Littletato hugged Julia tight and kissed her lips, smiling.
After that, Littletato grabbed her smartphone, she sent a message to Carol, her sister, on Vegesapp, asking what she was doing on Saturday.
Carol had blond hair, she said that she was just playing some Countable Vegestrike 1.6 and streaming it on Vegewitch.
Littletato said that it was very interesting, she asked for the Livestream link so she could watch it after watching the movie.
Carol sent the link of the stream to Littletato, Littletato said thanks with some happy face emojis, and said "Good game sis!"
Then Carol asked what Littletato was doing on Saturday.
Littletato said that she was watching a Marvel movie with her girlfriend Julia.
"What movie are you watching sis?" asked Carol.
"I'm watching 'The Vegengers: Infinite Vegetablewar'," replied Littletato.
"That's good, I still didn't watch it, I'm going to watch it after I finish my Livestream, good movie sis!" said Carol with some happy face emojis.
"Thanks, sis, hehe ^^," replied Littletato.
Then Littletato pressed play and relaxed on the couch, starting to watch the movie, the Marvel intro appeared on the screen.

The movie showed the Marvel logo, starting, it showed the spaceship of Vegethor in space.
A lot of Vegesgardians were dead on the spaceship, Vegebony Maw was walking among the corpses.
Vegeheimdall was badly wounded, he reached out trying to stop Vegebony Maw as he passed, but he lacks the strength.
Vegebony Maw stepped over the corpses with no mind as he spoke, as if they were scattered pieces of dirty clothing on a bedroom floor.
"Hear me, and rejoice. You have had the privilege of being saved by the Great Titan... You may think this is suffering... no. It is salvation.
Universal scales tip toward balance because of your sacrifice. Smile..." said Vegebony Maw, Corvus Glaive stabbed one of the lingering Vegesgardians, "For even in death, you have become Children of VegeThanos," continued Vegebony Maw.
Loki stayed with the Black Order. He watched VegeThanos, shrouded in darkness and light, a vague silhouette.
Some hours passed, the movie ended, Julia and Littletato loved the movie.
They were sad because of all the people that died at the hands of VegeThanos, just for universe balance, they wanted them to be revived.
Julia was sad because of Vegeter Parker that died, turning into ashes, Littletato was sad because of Mantis who turned into ashes.
Littletato hugged Julia tight and kissed her lips, the movie was marked as "Watched" in Littletato's profile of the Vegeflix app.
The couple was tired, Littletato turned off the TV and they both walked to the bedroom.
Julia and Littletato laid on the bed, Littletato covered her and Júlia with the blanket, they closed their eyes and slept in the cold night, hugging tight.

Chapter: 14 - A Happy New Year in 2019






It was a Sunday, in the year 2018, Littletato was working on her job on New Year's Eve, she could leave work early this day because of the New Year's Eve.
Littletato then grabbed her things and said happy new year to her coworker Mia.
She also stopped by her boss' room and wished a happy new year to her boss.
After that, Littletato left the building, it was a cold day in San Francisco, there was water all around the roads.
It was six in the afternoon.
Littletato was using her dark brown coat, she had an umbrella inside her purse if she needed it.
The girl started walking to her house, she was walking on the sidewalk.
It started raining, Littletato opened her purse and grabbed her umbrella, she untied it and opened it.
Then Littletato grabbed her smartphone from out of her purse and sent a message to Julia saying that she was going to be a little late because she was going to stop at the supermarket.
Julia replied saying okay, Littletato stored her smartphone in her purse again and started walking to the supermarket.
She arrived there and picked up a plastic basket and grabbed a Doritos pack, a bottle of 3,5 liters of Coca-cola, and a packet of chocolate stuffed biscuits.
Then Littletato started walking to the supermarket cashier, she paid for the purchase and left the supermarket.
After that, the girl continued walking home.

She arrived at her house's door, grabbing the house's key from her pocket and opening it.
Littletato entered the house and Julia hugged her, saying "Welcome home (okaeri), honey," while smiling.
Then Littletato kissed Julia's lips, "I'm back, honey," then she walked to the kitchen and left the plastic bags with the food on top of the table.
Julia started opening the plastic bags and taking the things off them.
"Oh, honey, you brought Doritos, I love them, for us to pass our New Year's Eve right?" asked Julia, smiling while holding the Doritos packet.
"Yes hon, I love it too, I also bought a big bottle of Coca-cola and a packet of chocolate stuffed biscuits," said Littletato, removing the Coca-cola bottle and the chocolate stuffed biscuits from the bags.
Then Littletato placed the bottle of Coca-cola inside the fridge for it to get cold.
She stored the Doritos packet and the chocolate stuffed biscuits packet inside the kitchen cabinet.
"Let's prepare ourselves for New Year's Eve hon?" asked Littletato.
"Yes hon, let's do it," replied Julia.
Then the couple walked to the bedroom and changed themselves, using white clothes for New Year's Eve.
"I heard that there is going to be a big screen with the countdown to the new year downtown on New Year's Eve," said Julia.
"Oh, that sounds good, let's watch a little movie and we're going there at eleven pm okay?" asked Littletato.
"Okay hon," replied Julia.

Then Littletato and Julia walked to the living room, they sat on the couch.
Littletato grabbed the TV controller and turned the TV on.
She started looking at the catalog of Vegeflix looking for a movie to watch.
(Vegeflix is a website and mobile app where you can watch series, movies, cartoons, and animes online, using a paid plan.)
Julia grabbed her smartphone and started sending messages to her friends wishing them a happy new year.
She sent messages to her sister Vitória, to Littletato's sister Carol, to Yam, and her mother and father.
They all replied, wishing Julia a happy new year, Julia also posted in her Vegesapp status wishing a happy new year to all of their contacts.
(Vegesapp is an app that you can install on your smartphone, it lets you chat with people, you need a phone number and a SIM card to use it.)
Littletato chose a movie for them to watch, it was called "The Vegengers: Vegend Game", it was a new superhero movie that launched recently.
Then Littletato grabbed her smartphone, she posted on her Vegesapp status wishing a happy new year to everyone.
After that, the girl sent messages to all of her friends wishing them a happy new year.
She said happy new year to Julia's sister Vitória, to her sister Carol, Yam, her coworker Mia, and her father and mother.
Then Littletato walked to the kitchen, grabbed Julia's water bottle, and walked to the living room, leaving it on top of the living room table at the right of the right arm of the couch.
After that, Littletato kissed Julia's lips and smiled, she walked to the kitchen and grabbed a bowl, opening the Doritos packet and throwing all of the Doritos inside the bowl.
Littletato asked from the kitchen if Julia wanted her to mix the Doritos and the chocolate stuffed biscuits on the bowl.
Julia replied saying yes, then Littletato opened the packet of biscuits and threw all of them inside the bowl.

Littletato had a Styrofoam box, she placed a lot of ice cubes inside it, then she grabbed two cups made of glass.
Then the girl grabbed the bottle of Coca-cola from inside the fridge's freezer and filled the two cups with Coca-cola.
After that, Littletato walked to the living room, leaving the cup of Julia next to her on the table at the right of the couch.
She left her cup on the left table that was on the left part of the couch.
Then Littletato placed the Coca-cola bottle inside the Styrofoam box filled with ice cubes so it does not get hot.
Littletato walked to the kitchen and grabbed the bowl, she turned the lights off and walked back to the living room.
After that, Littletato left the bowl of Doritos and chocolate stuffed biscuits between her and Julia.
Littletato grabbed the TV's controller and unpaused the movie, Julia posted on her Vegesapp status saying that she was going to watch a movie with Littletato before New Year's Eve.
Then Julia blocked her smartphone's screen, she kissed Littletato's lips and smiled.
The movie logo appeared, it was the Marvel Studios logo, the same company that made the "Vegeider-Tableman: Far From San Francisco" movie.
Julia grabbed some Doritos from the bowl and ate them, then she took a sip of her Coca-cola cup.
Littletato grabbed one Doritos and one chocolate stuffed biscuit from the bowl, she ate both of them and took a sip of her Coca-cola cup.
They continued watching the movie, the couple wanted to see the dead characters alive again, they were sad because they were gone.
At the half of the movie, there was half of the Doritos, half of the chocolate stuffed biscuits, and half of the Coca-cola bottle of 3,5 liters.

After watching for three hours, the movie ended, the food ended too, there was still some Coca-cola left in the bottle.
Littletato grabbed the bowl and brought it to the kitchen, she left it below the sink's tap and opened the tap.
Then she closed the tap and walked to the living room, sitting on the couch, Julia grabbed the two cups and left them on top of the sink.
Julia then came back to the living room, "Wanna end the rest, honey?" asked Littletato looking at the Coca-cola bottle.
"Yes," replied Julia grabbing the Coca-cola bottle and drinking from the beak.
Then they got ready for New Year's Eve, it was eleven and fifty o'clock at night.
Julia left the bottle of Coca-cola in the kitchen to put it in recycling the day after.
Littletato turned the TV off, the movie they watched was registered on the Watch History of Littletato's Vegeflix account.
The couple locked the house and started walking downtown to see the New Year's clock.
Both of them looked at the beautiful scenery, the trees, and the lights of the city of San Francisco.
There were a lot of people walking towards downtown to see the New Year Countdown.

After some minutes of walking, the couple arrived downtown.
A big crowd was there, the people were looking high at the big screen that was installed on a famous building in the city.
There were still eight minutes left to the New Year, the people watched the minutes pass on the digital display.
A lot of couples hugged tight and kissed, a lot of families hugged themselves.
It was a moment of happiness for everyone, everyone was in the spirit of Reveillon, making wishes for the New Year.
There were still five minutes left to the New Year, the people were looking at the big and high screen on the building.
Littletato thought about what she did this year after she met Julia and her life changed.
She thought about the friends that she made during this year after she moved to San Francisco and before.
About her first interview in San Francisco, she was happy thinking that she got a job at the Interworks Technologies company.
The girl thought about when she first met Julia at that coffee shop when she declared her love for Julia (chapter 1).
When she met her coworker, Littletato thought that she was kind and gentle (chapter 2).
That day that she bought the house, she was so happy that day, owning a house along with Julia (chapter 1).
Her various days going to work walking while listening to her folk playlist on the Vegetify app on her smartphone.
When Littletato met Julia's sister, Vitória, she was a designer, and a very interesting person (chapter 4).
That day when Littletato taught Julia to draw in the Paint Tool SAI program on her computer (chapter 5).
The dream she had about being a space traveler along with Julia (chapter 5).
When Littletato went to that park on Saturday and Yam appeared there, Littletato presented him to Julia, and then they went to the supermarket and bought a bottle of Coca-cola (chapter 6).
The Sunday when they played a lot of games in the Vegebox videogame that Littletato had, they played Vegetablefall 2 (chapter 7).
That Monday when she watched Captain Vegerica: Vegetable War with Julia while eating Doritos and drinking Coca-cola, it was very cool (chapter 8).
Her farm and rain dream, drinking a can of Coca-cola outside the old house, it started raining and she entered the house, wore some light clothes, and slept (chapter 9).
The allegoric dream with the Mexican man singing, the boy playing his electric guitar like a Dubstep bass, the gray-haired girl with the fridge, and the boy writing a story on his computer about a grape (chapter 10).
That dream she had about going on a trip to Texas with Julia, she woke up and did a lot of things, she watched an episode of Atypical with Julia (chapter 11).
When Littletato had a cookie factory and a cyberpunk dream, a dream about a cookie factory, and when she dreamt of that Castle of Glass and Twilight Sparkle (chapter 12).
That day when she watched The Vegengers: Infinite Vegetablewar with Julia, she posted the movie on her Vegesapp status (chapter 13).
Thirty seconds were remaining for the New Year, the crowd counted together.
Everyone shouting together, ten, nine, eight, seven, six, five, four, three, two, one.
There were fireworks on the big screen and real fireworks too, everyone shouted "Happy New Year! Happy 2019!"
Everyone was happy and smiling, looking at their relatives, their partners.
